                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1"> athātaḥ svabhāvaviprati<lb n="4"/>pattim
                        adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4"> svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśanām
                        manyathātvam maraṇāya tad yathā śuklā<cb n="1"/>nāṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ
                        kṛṣṇānā śuklatvaṃ | sthirāṇāṃ mṛdutvañ calānāñ calatvam acalānāñ
                        calatvam | pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ saṃkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutvaṃ | dī<cb
                            n="2"/>rghāṇāṃ hrasvaṃ vā hrasvānān dīrghatā |
                        apatanadharmmiṇām patanam akasmāc
                            chaityoṣṇasneharaukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇṇyā<lb n="5"/>ni
                        apasarpaṇam aṅgānāṃ svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ | śarīraikadeśānāṃm
                            avasraṃsotkṣiptabhrānta<unclear reason="overwriting"
                            >pati</unclear>tavimukt<unclear reason="faded"
                            >ā</unclear>ni<cb n="1"/>rgamātigamagurulaghutvāni
                        pravālavarṇṇavyaṅgaprādurbhāvo vākasmāt sirāṇāñ ca darśanaṃ lalāṭe
                        nāsāvaṃśe vā piṭako<cb n="2"/>tpattiḥ | udakotpattir netrarogaṃ
                        vināsrupravṛttir lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle svedapravṛttiḥ ||
                            gomaya<lb n="6"/>cūrṇṇaprakāśasya rajaso darśanam uttamāṅge
                        līyanam vā kapotakaṅkagṛdhraprabhṛtīnāṃ mūtrapurīṣapravṛddhi<cb
                            n="1"/>r abhuñjanānāṃ tanamūlahṛdayoḥ sūcaśūlotpattayaḥ |
                        madhye śūnatvam anteṣu parimlānayitvam | viparyayo vā
                            naṣṭahīnavikalavi<cb n="2"/>hṛtasvaram vā
                        vivarṇṇapuṣpaprādurbhāvo dantanakhaśarīreṣu yasya cāpsu
                        kaphaśakṛdretānsi nimajja<lb n="7"/>nti yasya ca dṛṣṭimaṇḍale
                        bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇy ālocyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo bhāti
                        yaś ca <cb n="1"/>durbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyāṃ pīḍyate |
                        kāsamānaś ca tṛṣṇātibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś chardibhaktadveṣayuktaḥ
                        saphenarudhirodvāmī hata<cb n="2"/>svaraḥ śūlābhihataś ca
                        manuṣyaśūnakaracaraṇonnadveṣī śasupiṇḍikānsapāṇipādaḥ | yaś ca <pb
                            n="27r"/><lb n="1"/>pūrvāhṇe bhuktam aparāhṇe śchardayaty
                        avidagdhaṃ sāryate vā jvarakāsārābhibhūtaḥ sa śvāsā mayate |
                        vastavad vi<cb n="1"/>lapamāno bhūmau patati | srastamuṣkaḥ
                        stabdhaśepo bhagnagrīvaḥ | praṇaṣṭamehaś ca manuṣyaḥ |
                        prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārdraśarī<cb n="1"/>raḥ | yaś ca loṣṭaṃ
                        loṣṭenābhihanti | kāṣṭhaṃ vā kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā cchinatti |
                        adharoṣṭham vā daśati | uttaro<lb n="1"/>ṣṭham vā leḍhi | āluñcati
                        karṇṇau keśāṃś ca | devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyāṃ vidveṣṭi yasya ca
                        vakrānuvakragā <cb n="1"/>grahā garhitasthānagatāḥ | janmaṛkṣam
                        vāsyolkāśanibhyām abhihanyate | rātrau vā
                            gṛhadvāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopa<cb n="2"
                        />karaṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbhāvo veti || </l>

                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">

                    <milestone facs="A 1267_11_29 (top image:l3:c2)" unit="folio"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part1"> vamanadravyāṇāṃ phalākhyānām madhye

                        bhavanti || tatra madanapuṣpāṇām ātapaśuṣkāṇāṃ cūrṇṇaṃ prakuṃcaṃ

                        pāyayitvā vāmayet | madanasalāṭūcūrṇṇāny evam madhulavaṇayuktāny

                        nirvṛttām vā nātiharitapāṇḍūnāṃ
                        kusumūṭāvavaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ ya<cb n="1"
                        />vavusamāṣasālyādidhānyarāśāv aṣṭarātroṣitaklinnabhinnānāṃ phalaṃ
                        pippalībhir āhṛtyātape pariśoṣayet tāsāṃ dadhipa<cb n="2"
                        />lavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ subhājanasthānām antarnakhamuṣṭhim uṣṇena
                        yaṣṭhīmadhukaṣāyeṇa kovidārā<lb n="5"/>dhvanyatamakaṣāyeṇa vā
                        vimṛdya trirātraparyuṣitaṃ madhusaindhavayuktam āsīrbhir
                        abhimantritam udanmu<cb n="1"/>khaḥ prāṅmukham āturaṃ pāyayed
                        anena mantreṇābhimantrya ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.1">brahmādakṣāsirudrendrabhūcandrārkānilānalāḥ |

                            jī<cb n="2"/>vantī kaṣāyeṇa pitte sthānagate |<g
